###########################
# Italian Events from scratch
###########################

add_namespace = ita
add_namespace = itafla
add_namespace = itasyn
add_namespace = itasoc
add_namespace = italib

### Introduction Event

country_event = {
	id = ita.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.0"}
	title = ita.0.t
	desc = ita.0.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ita.0.a
	}
}

country_event = { # Catholics complain
	id = ita.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.1"}
	title = ita.1.t
	desc = ita.1.d
	picture = ita_1

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		focus_progress = {
			focus = ITA_future_ppi
			progress > 0.2
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ita.1.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.02
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ita.1.b
		add_political_power = -25
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Farming Syndicates
	id = ita.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.3"}
	title = ita.3.t
	desc = ita.3.d
	picture = ita_3

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		focus_progress = {
			focus = ITA_future_ppi
			progress > 0.7
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = ita.3.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = revivalist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = ita.3.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = revivalist
			popularity = -0.02
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_purge_syndies_tip
		
		hidden_effect = {
			subtract_from_variable = { var = syndie_control value = 3 }
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ITA
					has_state_flag = ITA_state_syndie
				}
				clr_state_flag = ITA_state_syndie
				add_state_modifier = {
					modifier = { # Cant reset state modifiers so this adds the opposite effects to nullify the original
						local_building_slots = 1
						local_manpower = -0.1
						local_resources = -0.25
					}
				}					
			}		
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Fate of the PPI
	id = ita.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.4"}
	title = ita.4.t
	desc = ita.4.d
	picture = ita_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # pick conservatives
		name = ita.4.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fasci
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = collectivist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.25
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = social_conservative 
			long_name = ITA_social_democrat_party_long 
			name = ITA_social_democrat_party
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = social_democrat
			long_name = "Partito Socialista Democratico Italiano"
			name = "PSDI"
		}
		remove_every_minister = yes
		add_ideas = {
			ITA_Alcide_De_Gasperi_hog_sco
			ITA_Giuseppe_Pella_for_sco
			ITA_Giovanni_Gronchi_eco_sco
			ITA_Giovanni_Uberti_sec_sco
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_con_ppi
		add_coalition_social_democrat = yes 
		remove_ideas = ITA_ppi_stagnation
	}
	
	option = { # pick progressives 
		name = ita.4.b
		set_country_flag = ITA_prog_ppi
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		set_party_name = { 
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = "Democrazia Cristiana"
			name = "DC"
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		add_political_power = -50
		remove_ideas = ITA_ppi_stagnation
	}
}

country_event = { # random event selector for ITA_capitalists_support
	id = ita.7
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.7"}

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		focus_progress = {
			focus = ITA_capitalists_support
			progress > 0.5
		}	
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		random_list = {
			33 = {
				country_event = ita.8
			}
			33 = {
				country_event = ita.9
			}
			34 = {
				add_political_power = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # election events
	id = ita.14
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.14"}
	title = ita.14.t
	desc = ita.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_parliament

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		focus_progress = {
			focus = ITA_italian_election
			progress > 0.01
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 1 }

	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		# set up the variable starting values
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_commie
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_progressive
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_liberal
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_conservative
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_nationalist
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_progressive_vote
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_liberal_vote
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			var = ita_conservative_vote
			value = 0
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				country_event = { id = ita.221 days = 1825 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Commie
		name = ita.14.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_commie
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_democratic
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_fpick_com # Foreign minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_commie value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = collectivist popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = fasci popularity = 0.03 }
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = ITA_elecsupport_ussr }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ita.15
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Progressive
		name = ita.14.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		set_country_flag = ITA_fpick_sde # Foreign minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_progressive value = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_progressive_vote value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = ITA_elecsupport_ussrlight }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ita.15
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Liberal
		name = ita.14.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 15 }
		set_country_flag = ITA_fpick_lib # Foreign minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_liberal value = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_liberal_vote value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = market_liberal popularity = 0.05 }
		add_political_power = 50
		country_event = {
			id = ita.15
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Conservative
		name = ita.14.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		set_country_flag = ITA_fpick_con # Foreign minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_conservative value = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_conservative_vote value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_conservative popularity = 0.05 }
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_elecsupport_france }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ita.15
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Nationalist
		name = ita.14.f
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_revivalist
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_democratic
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_fpick_nat # Foreign minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_nationalist value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = national_populist popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = revivalist popularity = 0.03 }
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_neighbor_of = ITA
			}
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = ITA_electhreaten_us }
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ita.15
			hours = 12
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Economic reforms
	id = ita.17
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.17"}
	title = ita.17.t
	desc = ita.17.d
	picture = ita_17

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Commie
		name = ita.17.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 100
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_commie
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = ITA_rule_picked_democratic
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_epick_com # economic minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_commie value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = collectivist popularity = 0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = fasci popularity = 0.03 }
		random_owned_state = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = ita.18
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Progressive
		name = ita.17.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 40 }
		set_country_flag = ITA_epick_sde # economic minister candidate
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_progressive value = 1 }
		add_to_variable = {	var = ita_progressive_vote value = 1 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.05 }
		add_stability = 0.05
		country_event = {
			id = ita.18
			hours = 12
		}
	}
	option = { # Liberal
		name = ita.17.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 15 }
		set_country_flag = ITA_epick_lib # economic minister candidate

country_event = { # Commies win
	id = ita.20
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.20"}
	title = ita.20.t
	desc = ita.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_SRI_togliatti
	
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = ITA_election_over
		hidden_effect = {
			load_focus_tree = italy_socialist_economy
		}
	}	

	trigger = {
		original_tag = ITA
		has_country_flag = ITA_election_done
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = ITA_election_over
		}		
		OR = {
			check_variable = { ita_commie > 3 }
			AND = {
				check_variable = { ita_commie = 3 }
				check_variable = { ita_progressive < 3 }
				check_variable = { ita_liberal < 3 }
				check_variable = { ita_conservative < 3 }
				check_variable = { ita_nationalist < 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes

		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				party_popularity@collectivist > party_popularity@fasci 
			}
		}
		name = ita.20.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_com_win
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = collectivist
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		end_coalition = yes 
		add_coalition_fasci = yes 
		add_coalition_vanguardist = yes

      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Pompeo_Colajanni
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Ettore_Troilo
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Mario_Musolesi
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Pier_Luigi_Bellini_della_Stelle
        skill = 1
      }
			
      random_other_country = {
        news_event = { id = itanews.20 }
      }
			remove_every_minister = yes
			add_ideas = {
				ITA_Antonio_Gramsci_hog_col
				ITA_Vincenzo_Vacirca_for_col
				ITA_Achille_Grandi_eco_lib
				ITA_Vittorio_Vidali_sec_col
			}	
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { 
				party_popularity@fasci > party_popularity@collectivist 
			}
		}
		name = ita.20.a 
		set_country_flag = ITA_com_win
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fasci
		}
		add_political_power = 50
		end_coalition = yes 
		add_coalition_collectivist = yes 
		add_coalition_vanguardist = yes 
		hidden_effect = {
			add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Pompeo_Colajanni
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Ettore_Troilo
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Mario_Musolesi
        skill = 1
      }
      add_corps_commander_role = {
        character = ITA_Pier_Luigi_Bellini_della_Stelle
        skill = 1
      }
			
			ITA_Harukichi_Shimoi = { remove_unit_leader_role = yes }
			
			random_other_country = {
        news_event = { id = itanews.20 }
      }

	id = ita.32

	title = ita.32.t
	desc = ita.32.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	trigger = {
		original_tag = FRA
		ITA = {
			owns_state = 2
			NOT = {
				controls_state = 2
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
			OR = {
				has_war_with = PIE
				has_war_with = SIC
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = { # Yes
		name = ita.32.a
		set_country_flag = FRA_stole_ita
		add_political_power = -50
		#opinion_modifier
		
		every_state = { 
			limit = {
				is_owned_by = ITA
				NOT = {
					is_on_continent = europe
				}
			}
			set_state_flag = ITA_colonial_holding
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				LBA = {
					is_puppet_of = ITA
				}
			}
			every_state = { 
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = LBA
				}
				set_state_flag = ITA_colonial_holding
			}
		}
		
		# Libya
		if = {
			limit = {
				MOR = {
					is_puppet_of = FRA
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ITA
					is_on_continent = north_africa
				}
				MOR = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				MOR = {
					is_puppet_of = FRA
				}
				LBA = {
					is_puppet_of = ITA
				}
			}
			MOR = {
				annex_country = { target = LBA transfer_troops = no }
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {

						owns_state = 665
						owns_state = 458
					}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_owned_by = ITA
					is_on_continent = north_africa
				}
				FRA = {
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					OR = {
						owns_state = 665
						owns_state = 458
					}
				}
				LBA = {
					is_puppet_of = ITA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				annex_country = { target = LBA transfer_troops = no }
			}
		}
		
		# Italian Cameroon
		if = {
			limit = {
				NFQ = {
					is_puppet_of = FRA
				}
				ITA = {
					owns_state = 817
				}
			}
			NFQ = {
				transfer_state = 817
			}
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					owns_state = 539
				}
				ITA = {
					owns_state = 817
				}
			}

					owns_state = 345

		OR = {

country_event = { # Italy - What should we do about French states?
	id = ita.54
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.54"}
	title = ita.54.t
	desc = ita.54.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # push for compromise
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40 
			modifier = {
				factor = 8
				OR = {
					has_government = fasci
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = market_liberal
					has_government = social_conservative
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				ITA = {
					NOT = {
						is_in_faction_with = FRA
					}
				}
			}
		} 
		name = ita.54.a
		FRA = {
			country_event = ita.55
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Compromise is useless
		trigger = {
			ITA = {
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40 
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				OR = {
					has_government = revivalist
					has_government = national_populist
					has_government = collectivist
					has_government = vanguardist
				}
			}
		} 	
		name = ita.54.b
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_done_with_compromise }
			set_country_flag = ITA_france_conference_over
		}
		FRA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_done_with_compromise }
			remove_from_faction = ITA
			country_event = ita.193
		}
	}	
}

	id = ita.80
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.80"}
	title = ita.80.t
	desc = ita.80.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # We must leave the Entente
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_opinion = {
					target = FRA
					value < 0
				}
			}
		}	
		name = ita.80.a
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_no_compromise_from_france }
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_france_conference_over
		FRA = {
			remove_from_faction = ITA
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = ITA
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
			FRA = {
				remove_from_faction = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # we'll stay but we're not happy about it
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 4
				has_opinion = {
					target = FRA
					value > 49
				}
			}
		}	
		name = ita.80.b
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_no_compromise_from_france_light }
		}
		set_country_flag = ITA_france_conference_over
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_war_support = 0.1
	}	
}

				}

			}

			}

				}

			}
		}
	}

			}
		}	
		name = ita.134.a
	}
}

				}
			}			
		}

			limit = {
				ITA = {
					is_faction_leader = yes
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				add_to_faction = GRE
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}

				add_to_faction = GRE

		}
		else = {

country_event = { # Turkey - clear demil zone
	id = ita.169
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event ita.169"}

	trigger = {
		ITA = {
			has_country_flag = ITA_istanbul_nogo_zone
		}
		OR = {
			341 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
			347 = {
				is_demilitarized_zone = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			TUR = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							owns_state = 341
							owns_state = 347
						}
					}
					is_puppet_of = ITA
					is_in_faction_with = ITA
					has_war_with = ITA
				}
			}
			threat > 0.99
			ITA = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_puppet = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				341 = {
					is_demilitarized_zone = yes
				}
			}
			341 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				347 = {
					is_demilitarized_zone = yes
				}
			}
			347 = {
				set_demilitarized_zone = no
			}
		}		
	}
}

			}
		}
	}

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = itafla.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itafla.1"}
	title = itafla.1.t
	desc = itafla.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		date > 1936.10.0
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = itafla.1.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = revivalist
			popularity = 0.02
		}	
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = itafla.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itafla.2"}
	title = itafla.2.t
	desc = itafla.2.d
	picture = ita_16

	trigger = {
		tag = ITA
		date > 1936.5.0
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 7 }

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = itafla.2.a
		2 = {
			add_manpower = -1
		}	
	}
}

country_event = { # Fate of the Left
	id = itasoc.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasoc.2"}
	title = itasoc.2.t
	desc = itasoc.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Palmiro Togliatti wins
		name = itasoc.2.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_commies_picked
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = ITA_Palmiro_Togliatti
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = vanguardist_subtype
				traits = {}
			}
   		}
		remove_coalition_social_democrat = yes 
		remove_coalition_fasci = yes 
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = vanguardist
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = vanguardist
			last_election = "1934.3.26"
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		
		add_ideas = {
			ITA_Palmiro_Togliatti_hog_van
			ITA_Sergio_Panunzio_for_van
			ITA_Nicola_Bombacci_eco_van
			ITA_Ruggiero_Grieco_sec_van
			one_party_dictatorship
		}		
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = vanguardist
							has_government = collectivist
							has_government = fasci
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = itasoc.3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Bordiga wins
		name = itasoc.2.b
		set_country_flag = ITA_commies_picked
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes

			ruling_party = collectivist
			last_election = "1934.3.26"
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = no
		}

		add_ideas = {

			ITA_Vincenzo_Vacirca_for_col
			ITA_Alceste_De_Ambris_eco_col
			ITA_Vittorio_Vidali_sec_col
			workers_republic
		}		
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = vanguardist
							has_government = collectivist
							has_government = fasci
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = itasoc.3
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # Gramsci wins
		name = itasoc.2.c
		set_country_flag = ITA_commies_picked
		drop_cosmetic_tag = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = ITA_Antonio_Gramsci
			promote_leader = yes
			country_leader = {
				ideology = collectivist_subtype
				traits = {}
			}
		}
		remove_coalition_social_democrat = yes 
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = collectivist
			popularity = 0.05
		}

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = collectivist
			last_election = "1934.3.26"
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		
		add_ideas = {
			ITA_Antonio_Gramsci_hog_col
			ITA_Vincenzo_Vacirca_for_col
			ITA_Alceste_De_Ambris_eco_col
			ITA_Vittorio_Vidali_sec_col
			workers_republic
		}	
			
		if = {
			limit = {
				FRA = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_government = vanguardist
							has_government = collectivist
							has_government = fasci
						}
					}
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				country_event = itasoc.3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { # Matteotti wins
		name = itasoc.2.e

country_event = { # France kicks out commie italy
	id = itasoc.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasoc.3"}
	title = itasoc.3.t
	desc = itasoc.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = itasoc.3.a
		ITA = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = FRA modifier = ITA_expelled_by_france }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ITA = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				remove_from_faction = ITA
			}
		}
		
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = ITA
				is_in_faction_with = FRA
			}
			FRA = {
				remove_from_faction = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

			popularity = 0.02
		}
		21 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1

				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1

			}
		}	
	}
	
	option = {
		name = itasoc.4.b

		}

	}	
}

country_event = { # Soviets - Italy wants support
	id = itasoc.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasoc.5"}
	title = itasoc.5.t
	desc = itasoc.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # sure
		name = itasoc.5.a
		SOV = {
			add_opinion_modifier = { target = ITA modifier = ITA_agreed_to_support }
		}
		random_owned_controlled_state = {
			limit = {
				is_coastal = yes
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = dockyard
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = naval_doctrine
		}
		add_tech_bonus = {
			bonus = 0.5
			uses = 1
			category = naval_equipment
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = ITA_soviet_bonus
		ITA = {
			country_event = itasoc.6
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = itasoc.5.b
		add_political_power = 50
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = vanguardist
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		ITA = {
			country_event = itasoc.7
		}		
	}	
}

country_event = { #Italy - Pick Nat Pops or revivalists
	id = itasyn.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasyn.1"}
	title = itasyn.1.t
	desc = itasyn.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = itasyn.1.a
		set_country_flag = ITA_picked_nat_pops
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { ROOT.coalition_partners = token:revivalist }
				}
			}
			add_coalition_revivalist = yes 
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = national_populist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				ITA_Italo_Balbo_hog_npo
				ITA_Dino_Alfieri_for_npo
				ITA_Giuseppe_Volpi_eco_npo
				ITA_Alessandro_Pavolini_sec_npo
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = itasyn.1.b
		set_country_flag = ITA_picked_nat_syns
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					is_in_array = { ROOT.coalition_partners = token:national_populist }
				}
			}
			add_coalition_national_populist = yes 
		}		
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = revivalist
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = revivalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = {
				ITA_Gabriele_Annunzio_hog_val
				ITA_Giacomo_Acerbo_for_val
				ITA_Edmondo_Rossoni_eco_val
				ITA_Luigi_Razza_sec_val
			}
		}
	}	
}

      character = ITA_Arengo_del_Italia

        ideology = revivalist_subtype
        traits = {}
      }
    }
		hidden_effect = {
			ITA = {
				country_event = {

					days = 30
				}
			}

country_event = { #Italy - Italo-Soviet Friendship Pact?
	id = itasyn.5
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasyn.5"}
	title = itasyn.5.t
	desc = itasyn.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = ITA
		AND = {
			SOV = {
				exists = yes
			}
			ITA = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # send the offer
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 160
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio < 1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2			
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value > 25
				}
			}
		}
		name = itasyn.5.a
		SOV = {
			country_event = itasyn.6
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # USSR isn't worth our time
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = SOV
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2			
				has_opinion = {
					target = SOV
					value < -25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2			
				SOV = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}
		name = itasyn.5.b
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = SOV modifier = ITA_denounces_us }		
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.05
	}		
}

	trigger = {
		original_tag = ITA
		has_country_flag = ITA_revivalist_sov_pact
		ITA = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				is_faction_leader = yes
			}
			NOT = {
				has_war_with = SOV
			}
		}
		OR = {
			threat > 0.5
			GER = {
				OR = {
					has_war_with = FRA
					has_war_with = ENG
					has_war_with = SOV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = { # send the offer
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}	
		name = itasyn.9.a
		SOV = {
			country_event = itasyn.10
		}
	}	
	
	option = { # USSR isn't worth our time
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}	
		name = itasyn.9.b	
		add_political_power = 25
		add_stability = 0.05
	}		
}

country_event = { #USSR - Italo-Soviet alliance?
	id = itasyn.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event itasyn.10"}
	title = itasyn.10.t
	desc = itasyn.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ITA_firenze

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 160
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = ITA
					ratio < 1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2			
				has_opinion = {
					target = ITA
					value > 25
				}
			}
		}
		name = itasyn.10.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					ITA = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = ITA
					}
					set_country_flag = ITA_italian_ally
				}
			}
			ITA = {
				create_faction = "Rome-Moscow Axis"
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ITA_italian_ally
				}
				ITA = {
					add_to_faction = PREV
				}
			}
			
			if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction_with = SOV
					}
					ITA = {
						add_to_faction = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			
			ITA = {
				add_to_faction = SOV
			}
			
			ITA = {
				country_event = itasyn.11
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = { # no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = ITA
					ratio > 1
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 1.5			
				has_opinion = {
					target = ITA
					value < -25
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2			
				ITA = {
					is_major = no
				}
			}
		}	
		name = itasyn.10.b		
		add_political_power = 25
		ITA = {
			country_event = itasyn.12
		}		
	}		
}
